	measure 'Volume FCST Act' = ```
			
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(TODAY())
			VAR CurrentYear = YEAR(TODAY())
			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			
			RETURN
			IF (
			    VisualYear = CurrentYear,
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			
			        // Q1: Jan–Mar → Show AOP for ALL months
			        CurrentMonth IN {2,3,4},
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtAOP]),
			            'V_Dim_FB_PlHier'[PlSubHier]  IN { "Franchise cases", "Contract cases" }
			        ),
			
			        // Q2: Apr–Jun → Custom logic
			        CurrentMonth IN {5,6,7},
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtFcst39]),
			           'V_Dim_FB_PlHier'[PlSubHier]  IN { "Franchise cases", "Contract cases" },
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 4,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 7,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtFcst39]),
			           'V_Dim_FB_PlHier'[PlSubHier]  IN { "Franchise cases", "Contract cases" },
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 7
			       ),
			
			        // Q3: Jul–Sep → Show FCST_66 from July to Dec
			        CurrentMonth IN {8,9,10},
			       CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst66]),
			           'V_Dim_FB_PlHier'[PlSubHier]  IN { "Franchise cases", "Contract cases" },
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 7,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 8,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst66]),
			          'V_Dim_FB_PlHier'[PlSubHier]  IN { "Franchise cases", "Contract cases" },
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 8
			       ),
			
			        // Q4: Oct–Dec → Show FCST_93 from October to Dec
			        CurrentMonth IN {11,12,1},
			         CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93]),
			            'V_Dim_FB_PlHier'[PlSubHier]  IN { "Franchise cases", "Contract cases" },
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 10,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 11,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93]),
			           'V_Dim_FB_PlHier'[PlSubHier]  IN { "Franchise cases", "Contract cases" },
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >=11
			       )
			    )
			)
			
			
			```

	measure 'OI FCST Act' = ```
			
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(TODAY())
			VAR CurrentYear = YEAR(TODAY())
			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			 
			RETURN
			IF (
			    VisualYear = CurrentYear,
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			 
			        // Q1: Jan–Mar → Show AOP for ALL months
			        CurrentMonth IN {2,3,4},
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtAOP]),
			           V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] IN {"Total Operating Expense","Gross Profit","Other Income (Expense)"}
			        ),
			 
			        // Q2: Apr–Jun → Custom logic
			        CurrentMonth IN {5,6,7},
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtFcst39]),
			           V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] IN {"Total Operating Expense","Gross Profit","Other Income (Expense)"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 4,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 7,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtFcst39]),
			           V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] IN {"Total Operating Expense","Gross Profit","Other Income (Expense)"},
			           'V_Dim_FB_Opex'[OpexLine] IN {"Total COGS","DSD-T&W"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 7,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y"
			           
			       ),
			 
			        // Q3: Jul–Sep → Show FCST_66 from July to Dec
			        CurrentMonth IN {8,9,10},
			       CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst66]),
			          V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] IN {"Total Operating Expense","Gross Profit","Other Income (Expense)"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 7,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 8,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst66]),
			            V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] IN {"Total Operating Expense","Gross Profit","Other Income (Expense)"},
			           'V_Dim_FB_Opex'[OpexLine] IN {"Total COGS","DSD-T&W"},
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 8
			       ),
			 
			        // Q4: Oct–Dec → Show FCST_93 from October to Dec
			        CurrentMonth IN {11,12,1},
			         CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93]),
			          V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] IN {"Total Operating Expense","Gross Profit","Other Income (Expense)"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 10,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 11,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93]),
			            V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] IN {"Total Operating Expense","Gross Profit","Other Income (Expense)"},
			           'V_Dim_FB_Opex'[OpexLine] IN {"Total COGS","DSD-T&W"},
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >=11
			       )
			    )
			)

	measure Volume_AttainmentSelected =

			    TRUE(),
			SelectedToggle = "Absolute" && SelectedScenario = "AOP", [Arrow to Vol_AOP],
			SelectedToggle = "Absolute" && SelectedScenario = "FCST", [Arrow to Vol_FCST],
			SelectedToggle = "Absolute" && SelectedScenario = "YA", [Arrow to Vol_PY],
			SelectedToggle = "RPC" && SelectedScenario = "AOP", [Arrow to Vol_AOP],
			SelectedToggle = "RPC" && SelectedScenario = "FCST", [Arrow to Vol_FCST],
			SelectedToggle = "RPC" && SelectedScenario = "YA", [Arrow to Vol_PY]
			)

	measure 'Colour Format Volume' =
			
			VAR ComparisonType = SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics])
			VAR ToggleType = SELECTEDVALUE('Abs/RPC Table'[Abs/RPC])
			
			-- Select value based on toggle and scenario
			VAR VarValue =
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        ToggleType = "Absolute" && ComparisonType = "AOP", [Volume Varient AOP],
			        ToggleType = "Absolute" && ComparisonType = "FCST",[Volume Varient FCST],
			        ToggleType = "Absolute" && ComparisonType = "YA",[Volume Varient PY],
			        ToggleType = "RPC" && ComparisonType = "AOP", [Volume Varient AOP],
			        ToggleType = "RPC" && ComparisonType = "FCST",[Volume Varient FCST],
			        ToggleType = "RPC" && ComparisonType = "YA",[Volume Varient PY]
			    )
			
			-- Return the color
			RETURN
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        VarValue > 0, "#348939",              -- Green
			        VarValue < 0, "#9B1D1E"            -- Red
			    )

			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 8
			       ),
			 
			        // Q4: Oct–Dec → Show FCST_93 from October to Dec
			        CurrentMonth IN {11,12,1},
			         CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93]),
			          V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] IN {"Total Operating Expense","Gross Profit","Other Income (Expense)"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 10,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 11,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93]),
			            V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] IN {"Total Operating Expense","Gross Profit","Other Income (Expense)"},
			           'V_Dim_FB_Opex'[OpexLine] IN {"Total COGS","DSD-T&W"},
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >=11
			       )
			    )
			)
			```
		lineageTag: 22336868-02de-4632-98b2-804ce45a8cb7

	measure OI_Bar_Act =

			    SUM(V_FB_Financial_Management[AmtAct]),
			    V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] IN {"Total Operating Expense","Gross Profit","Other Income (Expense)"},
			    FILTER(
			        VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]),
			        YEAR(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]) = YEAR(TODAY()) &&
			        MONTH(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]) <= MONTH(TODAY())-1

	measure Volume_Bar_Actual_Selected =
			
			VAR SelectedToggle = SELECTEDVALUE('Abs/RPC Table'[Abs/RPC], "Absolute")
			VAR TodayDate = TODAY()
			VAR DataDate = MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]) -- Assuming this is the date context of the data
			VAR UnlockDate = DATE(YEAR(DataDate), MONTH(DataDate) + 1, 7)
			
			RETURN
			IF (
			    TodayDate >= UnlockDate,
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        SelectedToggle = "Absolute", [Volume_Bar_Act],
			        SelectedToggle = "RPC", [Volume_Bar_Act]
			    ),
			    BLANK()
			)

	measure 'TableArrow to Vol_AOP' = ```
			
			VAR VarPercent = [Volume Varient AOP%]
			VAR FormattedPercent =
			    IF(
			        VarPercent < 0,
			        "(" & FORMAT(ABS(VarPercent), "0%") & ")",
			        FORMAT(VarPercent, "0%")
			    )
			VAR Arrow =
			    IF(
			        VarPercent < 0,
			        " " & UNICHAR(9660)
			    )
			
			RETURN

			VAR ComparisonType = SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics])

			        ToggleType = "Absolute" && ComparisonType = "FCST",[GP Varient FCST%],
			        ToggleType = "Absolute" && ComparisonType = "YA",[GP Varient PY%],

			        ToggleType = "RPC" && ComparisonType = "FCST",[GP Varient RPC FCST%],

			-- Return the color
			RETURN
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        VarValue > 0, "#000000",            
			        VarValue < 0, "#9B1D1E"         
			    )
			```

	measure 'SG&A Labor FCST' = ```
			
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(TODAY())
			VAR CurrentYear = YEAR(TODAY())
			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			
			RETURN
			IF (
			    VisualYear = CurrentYear,
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			
			        // Q1: Jan–Mar → Show AOP for ALL months
			        CurrentMonth IN {2,3,4},
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtAOP]),
			             V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"}
			        ),
			
			        // Q2: Apr–Jun → Custom logic
			        CurrentMonth IN {5,6,7},
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtFcst39]),
			            V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 4,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 7,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtFcst39]),
			            V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 7
			       ),
			
			        // Q3: Jul–Sep → Show FCST_66 from July to Dec
			        CurrentMonth IN {8,9,10},
			       CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst66]),
			            V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 7,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 8,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst66]),
			           V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 8
			       ),
			
			        // Q4: Oct–Dec → Show FCST_93 from October to Dec
			        CurrentMonth IN {11,12,1},
			         CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93]),
			             V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 10,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 11,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93]),
			           V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >=11
			       )
			    )
			)

		formatStringDefinition =
				VAR NonDSDValue = [Non Labor opex_KPI]
				VAR SelectedToggle = SELECTEDVALUE('Abs/RPC Table'[Abs/RPC], "Absolute")
				VAR FormatString =
				SWITCH(
				        SelectedToggle,
				        "Absolute",
				            SWITCH(
				                TRUE(),
				                NonDSDValue >= 1000000, "$#,##0,,.0M",
				                NonDSDValue >= 1000, "$#,##0,.0K",
				                NonDSDValue < 1000, "$#,##0.0"
				            ),
				        "RPC", "$#,##0.00",
				        BLANK()
				    )
				
				RETURN
				FormatString

	measure 'Colour Format Total Labor' =

			VAR VarValue =
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        ToggleType = "Absolute" && ComparisonType = "AOP", [Total Labor Varient AOP],
			        ToggleType = "Absolute" && ComparisonType = "FCST",[Total Labor Varient FCST],
			        ToggleType = "Absolute" && ComparisonType = "YA",[Total Labor Varient PY],
			        ToggleType = "RPC" && ComparisonType = "AOP", [Total Labor Varient RPC AOP],
			        ToggleType = "RPC" && ComparisonType = "FCST",[Total Labor Varient RPC FCST],
			        ToggleType = "RPC" && ComparisonType = "YA",[Total Labor Varient RPC PY]
			    )
			
			-- Return the color
			RETURN
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        VarValue > 0, "#348939",              -- Green
			        VarValue < 0, "#9B1D1E"            -- Red
			    )

	measure 'Revenue_Monthly_FCST dummy' =
			
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(TODAY())
			
			VAR ForecastMeasure =
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        CurrentMonth <= 3, sum('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtAop]) ,
			        CurrentMonth <= 6, sum('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst39]),
			        CurrentMonth <= 9, sum('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst66]),
			        TRUE, sum('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93])
			    )
			
			RETURN
			    CALCULATE(
			        (ForecastMeasure),
			        V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] IN {"Net Sales"},
			        YEAR(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]) = YEAR(TODAY())
			    )
		lineageTag: 9f5bcb07-978e-4115-9285-ad88f68af978

	measure 'SG&A NON Labor FCST' = ```
			
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(TODAY())
			VAR CurrentYear = YEAR(TODAY())
			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			
			RETURN
			IF (
			    VisualYear = CurrentYear,
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			
			        // Q1: Jan–Mar → Show AOP for ALL months
			        CurrentMonth IN {2,3,4},
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtAOP]),
			            V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"}
			        ),
			
			        // Q2: Apr–Jun → Custom logic
			        CurrentMonth IN {5,6,7},
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtFcst39]),
			           V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 4,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 7,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtFcst39]),
			           V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 7
			       ),
			
			        // Q3: Jul–Sep → Show FCST_66 from July to Dec
			        CurrentMonth IN {8,9,10},
			       CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst66]),
			           V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 7,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 8,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst66]),
			          V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 8
			       ),
			
			        // Q4: Oct–Dec → Show FCST_93 from October to Dec
			        CurrentMonth IN {11,12,1},
			         CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93]),
			            V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 10,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 11,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93]),
			          V_Dim_FB_Opex[OpexLine] = "SG&A",
			        V_Dim_FB_Company[CmpnyCode] IN {"1010","1000"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >=11
			       )
			    )

	measure 'DSD Labor FCST' = ```
			
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(TODAY())
			VAR CurrentYear = YEAR(TODAY())
			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			
			RETURN
			IF (
			    VisualYear = CurrentYear,
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			
			        // Q1: Jan–Mar → Show AOP for ALL months
			        CurrentMonth IN {2,3,4},
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtAOP]),
			            V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] = "Total Operating Expense",
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"}
			        ),
			
			        // Q2: Apr–Jun → Custom logic
			        CurrentMonth IN {5,6,7},
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtFcst39]),
			           V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] = "Total Operating Expense",
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 4,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 7,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_financial_Management'[AmtFcst39]),
			          V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] = "Total Operating Expense",
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 7
			       ),
			
			        // Q3: Jul–Sep → Show FCST_66 from July to Dec
			        CurrentMonth IN {8,9,10},
			       CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst66]),
			          V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] = "Total Operating Expense",
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 7,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 8,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst66]),
			          V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] = "Total Operating Expense",
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 8
			       ),
			
			        // Q4: Oct–Dec → Show FCST_93 from October to Dec
			        CurrentMonth IN {11,12,1},
			         CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93]),
			            V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] = "Total Operating Expense",
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >= 10,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < 11,
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "N"
			        ) +
			        CALCULATE(
			            SUM('V_FB_Financial_Management'[AmtFcst93]),
			           V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] = "Total Operating Expense",
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlSubHier] IN {"Labor", "Benefits"},
			        NOT V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"},
			            'V_FB_financial_Management'[IsForecast] = "Y",
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] >=11
			       )

	measure Total_Breakage_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_Table = ```
			
			VAR TodayDate = TODAY()
			VAR CurrentMonthStart = DATE(YEAR(TodayDate), MONTH(TodayDate), 1)
			VAR DelayCutoff = CurrentMonthStart + 6  // 7th of the current month
			
			VAR MaxClosedMonth =
			    EOMONTH(TodayDate, IF(TodayDate < DelayCutoff, -2, -1))
			
			VAR CurrentYear = YEAR(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			VAR VisualQuarter = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter])
			VAR IsCurrentYear = VisualYear = CurrentYear
			
			VAR ExpectedMonths = IF(IsCurrentYear, CurrentMonth, 12)
			
			VAR SelectedMonths =
			    CALCULATETABLE(
			        VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = VisualYear
			    )
			
			VAR TotalMonthsSelected = COUNTROWS(SelectedMonths)
			VAR IsFullPeriod = TotalMonthsSelected = ExpectedMonths
			
			VAR IsDateSelected =
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Month]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate])
			
			VAR MaxClosedQuarter =
			    CALCULATE(
			        MAX('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth,
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = CurrentYear
			    )
			
			VAR IsClosedQuarter =
			    VisualYear < CurrentYear ||
			    (VisualYear = CurrentYear && VisualQuarter < MaxClosedQuarter)
			
			VAR slicerFilter =
			    FILTER(
			        ALLSELECTED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth
			    )
			
			VAR MetricSelected = SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics])
			VAR BaseMeasure = [Total_Breakage_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_Table_final]
			VAR FilteredMeasure = CALCULATE(BaseMeasure, slicerFilter)
			
			RETURN
			    IF (
			        MetricSelected = "FCST",
			        IF (
			            IsDateSelected && NOT IsFullPeriod && NOT IsClosedQuarter,
			            IF(FilteredMeasure <> 0, FilteredMeasure, BLANK()),
			            BLANK()
			        ),
			        BaseMeasure
			    )
			
			
			
			
			/*IF(
			    SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics]) = "FCST",
			    IF(
			        MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber])<=6,"",[Total_Breakage_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_Table_final]),
			    [Total_Breakage_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_Table_final])*/
			    
			```
		formatString: #,##0%;(#,##0%)
		displayFolder: Ops
		lineageTag: a97eddce-2579-4cca-be3e-18c1c92f9d99

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isCustom":true}

	measure Shrinklescence_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_Table =
			
			VAR TodayDate = TODAY()
			VAR CurrentMonthStart = DATE(YEAR(TodayDate), MONTH(TodayDate), 1)
			VAR DelayCutoff = CurrentMonthStart + 6  // 7th of the current month
			
			VAR MaxClosedMonth =
			    EOMONTH(TodayDate, IF(TodayDate < DelayCutoff, -2, -1))
			
			VAR CurrentYear = YEAR(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			VAR VisualQuarter = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter])
			VAR IsCurrentYear = VisualYear = CurrentYear
			
			VAR ExpectedMonths = IF(IsCurrentYear, CurrentMonth, 12)
			
			VAR SelectedMonths =
			    CALCULATETABLE(
			        VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = VisualYear
			    )
			
			VAR TotalMonthsSelected = COUNTROWS(SelectedMonths)
			VAR IsFullPeriod = TotalMonthsSelected = ExpectedMonths
			
			VAR IsDateSelected =
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Month]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate])
			
			VAR MaxClosedQuarter =
			    CALCULATE(
			        MAX('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth,
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = CurrentYear
			    )
			
			VAR IsClosedQuarter =
			    VisualYear < CurrentYear ||
			    (VisualYear = CurrentYear && VisualQuarter < MaxClosedQuarter)
			
			VAR slicerFilter =
			    FILTER(
			        ALLSELECTED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth
			    )
			
			VAR MetricSelected = SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics])
			VAR BaseMeasure = MAX(-10, MIN([Shrinklescence_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_Table_final], 10))
			VAR FilteredMeasure = CALCULATE(BaseMeasure, slicerFilter)
			
			RETURN
			    IF (
			        MetricSelected = "FCST",
			        IF (
			            IsDateSelected && NOT IsFullPeriod && NOT IsClosedQuarter,
			            IF(FilteredMeasure <> 0, FilteredMeasure, BLANK()),
			            BLANK()
			        ),
			        BaseMeasure
			    )
			/*IF(
			    SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics]) = "FCST",
			    IF(
			        MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber])<=6,BLANK(),[Shrinklescence_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_Table_final]),
			  MAX(-10, MIN([Shrinklescence_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_Table_final], 10))
			
			    )*/
		displayFolder: Ops
		lineageTag: 1b272d56-4e3f-45b9-9325-6be845d19f42

		formatStringDefinition = "#,##0%;(#,##0%)"

	measure Selected_Period = ```
			
			VAR _isWeek =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[WeekStarting_ISO]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthDesc]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isMonth =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthDesc]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			RETURN 
			SWITCH(
			    TRUE(),
			    _isWeek, [Date Validation_Day],
			    _isMonth, [Date Validation_Month],
			    _isQuarter,[Date Validation_Quarter],
			    _isYear, [Date Validation_Year],
			    BLANK()
			)
			
			
			/*
			SWITCH(
			    TRUE(),
			   _isWeek, VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[WeekStarting_ISO]),
			   _isMonth, VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfMonth]),
			   _isQuarter, VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]),
			    _isYear, VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]),
			    BLANK()
			)
			*/
			```
		displayFolder: Ops - DNP

	measure Total_Breakage_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_UI = ```
			
			VAR TodayDate = TODAY()
			VAR CurrentMonthStart = DATE(YEAR(TodayDate), MONTH(TodayDate), 1)
			VAR DelayCutoff = CurrentMonthStart + 6  // 7th of the current month
			
			VAR MaxClosedMonth =
			    EOMONTH(TodayDate, IF(TodayDate < DelayCutoff, -2, -1))
			
			VAR CurrentYear = YEAR(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			VAR VisualQuarter = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter])
			VAR IsCurrentYear = VisualYear = CurrentYear
			
			VAR ExpectedMonths = IF(IsCurrentYear, CurrentMonth, 12)
			
			VAR SelectedMonths =
			    CALCULATETABLE(
			        VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = VisualYear
			    )
			
			VAR TotalMonthsSelected = COUNTROWS(SelectedMonths)
			VAR IsFullPeriod = TotalMonthsSelected = ExpectedMonths
			
			VAR IsDateSelected =
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Month]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate])
			
			VAR MaxClosedQuarter =
			    CALCULATE(
			        MAX('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth,
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = CurrentYear
			    )
			
			VAR IsClosedQuarter =
			    VisualYear < CurrentYear ||
			    (VisualYear = CurrentYear && VisualQuarter < MaxClosedQuarter)
			
			VAR slicerFilter =
			    FILTER(
			        ALLSELECTED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth
			    )
			
			VAR MetricSelected = SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics])
			VAR BaseMeasure = [Total_Breakage_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops]
			VAR FilteredMeasure = CALCULATE(BaseMeasure, slicerFilter)
			
			RETURN
			    IF (
			        MetricSelected = "FCST",
			        IF (
			            IsDateSelected && NOT IsFullPeriod && NOT IsClosedQuarter,
			            IF(FilteredMeasure <> 0, FilteredMeasure, BLANK()),
			            BLANK()
			        ),
			        BaseMeasure
			    )
			
			
			
			
			
			/*IF(
			    SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics]) = "FCST",
			    IF(
			        MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber])<=6,"",
			        [Total_Breakage_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops]),
			    [Total_Breakage_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops])*/
			    
			
			```
		displayFolder: Ops
		lineageTag: 495eb4eb-db22-44f6-8441-693c4f559d36

		formatStringDefinition = "#,##0%;(#,##0%)"

	measure Obsolescence_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_UI = ```
			
			VAR TodayDate = TODAY()
			VAR CurrentMonthStart = DATE(YEAR(TodayDate), MONTH(TodayDate), 1)
			VAR DelayCutoff = CurrentMonthStart + 6  // 7th of the current month
			
			VAR MaxClosedMonth =
			    EOMONTH(TodayDate, IF(TodayDate < DelayCutoff, -2, -1))
			
			VAR CurrentYear = YEAR(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			VAR VisualQuarter = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter])
			VAR IsCurrentYear = VisualYear = CurrentYear
			
			VAR ExpectedMonths = IF(IsCurrentYear, CurrentMonth, 12)
			
			VAR SelectedMonths =
			    CALCULATETABLE(
			        VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = VisualYear
			    )
			
			VAR TotalMonthsSelected = COUNTROWS(SelectedMonths)
			VAR IsFullPeriod = TotalMonthsSelected = ExpectedMonths
			
			VAR IsDateSelected =
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Month]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate])
			
			VAR MaxClosedQuarter =
			    CALCULATE(
			        MAX('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth,
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = CurrentYear
			    )
			
			VAR IsClosedQuarter =
			    VisualYear < CurrentYear ||
			    (VisualYear = CurrentYear && VisualQuarter < MaxClosedQuarter)
			
			VAR slicerFilter =
			    FILTER(
			        ALLSELECTED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth
			    )
			
			VAR MetricSelected = SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics])
			VAR BaseMeasure = [Obsolescence_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops]
			VAR FilteredMeasure = CALCULATE(BaseMeasure, slicerFilter)
			
			RETURN
			    IF (
			        MetricSelected = "FCST",
			        IF (
			            IsDateSelected && NOT IsFullPeriod && NOT IsClosedQuarter,
			            IF(FilteredMeasure <> 0, FilteredMeasure, BLANK()),
			            BLANK()
			        ),
			        BaseMeasure
			    )
			/*IF(
			    SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics]) = "FCST",
			    IF(
			        MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber])<=6,"",[Obsolescence_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops]),
			    [Obsolescence_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops])*/
			    
			// var _x = [Obsolescence_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops]
			// RETURN 
			// IF(
			//     _x>0, 
			//         _x,
			//         IF(
			//             _x<0,
			//                 _x*(-1),
			//                 _X
			//         )
			// )
			```

	measure 'Conditional_Volume AttainmentSelected' = ```
			
			VAR SelectedScenario = SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics], "AOP")
			VAR SelectedToggle = SELECTEDVALUE('Abs/RPC Table'[Abs/RPC], "Absolute")
			VAR TodayDate = TODAY()
			VAR CurrentMonthStart = DATE(YEAR(TodayDate), MONTH(TodayDate), 1)
			VAR DelayCutoff = CurrentMonthStart + 6  -- 7th of current month
			VAR MaxClosedMonth =
			    IF(
			        TodayDate < DelayCutoff,
			        EOMONTH(TodayDate, -2),  // Treat two months ago as last closed
			        EOMONTH(TodayDate, -1)   // Otherwise, use last month
			    )
			
			VAR Currentyear = YEAR(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			VAR IsCurrentYear = VisualYear = YEAR(MaxClosedMonth)
			
			VAR ExpectedMonths =
			    IF(IsCurrentYear, CurrentMonth, 12)
			
			VAR SelectedMonths =
			    CALCULATETABLE(
			        VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = VisualYear
			    )
			
			VAR TotalMonthsSelected = COUNTROWS(SelectedMonths)
			VAR IsFullPeriod = TotalMonthsSelected = ExpectedMonths
			
			VAR IsDateSelected =
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Month]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate])
			
			VAR slicerFilter =
			    FILTER(
			        ALLSELECTED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth
			    )
			
			RETURN
			SWITCH(
			    TRUE(),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "Absolute" && SelectedScenario = "AOP",
			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([Volume Varient AOP%], slicerFilter)
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "Absolute" && SelectedScenario = "FCST",
			    IF(IsDateSelected && NOT IsFullPeriod,
			        CALCULATE([Volume Varient FCST%], slicerFilter),
			        BLANK()
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "Absolute" && SelectedScenario = "YA",
			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([Volume Varient PY%], slicerFilter)
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "RPC" && SelectedScenario = "AOP",
			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([Volume Varient AOP%], slicerFilter)
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "RPC" && SelectedScenario = "FCST",
			    IF(IsDateSelected && NOT IsFullPeriod,
			        CALCULATE([Volume Varient FCST%], slicerFilter),
			        BLANK()
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "RPC" && SelectedScenario = "YA",
			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([Volume Varient PY%], slicerFilter)
			    ),
			
			    BLANK()
			)
			
			```
		formatString: #,##0%;(#,##0%)

			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			VAR IsCurrentYear = VisualYear = YEAR(MaxClosedMonth)
			
			VAR ExpectedMonths =
			    IF(IsCurrentYear, CurrentMonth, 12)
			
			VAR SelectedMonths =
			    CALCULATETABLE(
			        VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = VisualYear
			    )
			
			VAR TotalMonthsSelected = COUNTROWS(SelectedMonths)
			VAR IsFullPeriod = TotalMonthsSelected = ExpectedMonths
			
			VAR IsDateSelected =
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Month]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate])
			
			VAR slicerFilter =
			    FILTER(
			        ALLSELECTED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth
			    )
			
			RETURN
			MAX(-10,MIN(
			SWITCH(
			    TRUE(),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "Absolute" && SelectedScenario = "AOP",
			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([OI Varient AOP%], slicerFilter)
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "Absolute" && SelectedScenario = "FCST",
			    IF(IsDateSelected && NOT IsFullPeriod,
			        CALCULATE([OI Varient FCST%], slicerFilter),
			        BLANK()
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "Absolute" && SelectedScenario = "YA",
			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([OI Varient PY%], slicerFilter)
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "RPC" && SelectedScenario = "AOP",
			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([OI Varient RPC AOP%], slicerFilter)
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "RPC" && SelectedScenario = "FCST",
			    IF(IsDateSelected && NOT IsFullPeriod,
			        CALCULATE([OI Varient RPC FCST%], slicerFilter),
			        BLANK()

			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([OI Varient RPC PY%], slicerFilter)

			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([T&W Fleet Varient RPC PY%], slicerFilter)
			    ),
			
			    BLANK()
			)
			
			
			
			
			
			
			
			
			
			
			
			```

	measure 'Conditional NSG_new' = ```
			
			VAR SelectedScenario = SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics], "AOP")
			VAR SelectedToggle = SELECTEDVALUE('Abs/RPC Table'[Abs/RPC], "Absolute")
			VAR TodayDate = TODAY()
			VAR CurrentMonthStart = DATE(YEAR(TodayDate), MONTH(TodayDate), 1)
			VAR DelayCutoff = CurrentMonthStart + 6  -- 7th of current month
			VAR MaxClosedMonth =
			    IF(
			        TodayDate < DelayCutoff,
			        EOMONTH(TodayDate, -2),  // Treat two months ago as last closed
			        EOMONTH(TodayDate, -1)   // Otherwise, use last month
			    )
			
			VAR Currentyear = YEAR(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			VAR IsCurrentYear = VisualYear = YEAR(MaxClosedMonth)
			
			VAR ExpectedMonths =
			    IF(IsCurrentYear, CurrentMonth, 12)
			
			VAR SelectedMonths =
			    CALCULATETABLE(
			        VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = VisualYear
			    )
			
			VAR TotalMonthsSelected = COUNTROWS(SelectedMonths)
			VAR IsFullPeriod = TotalMonthsSelected = ExpectedMonths
			
			VAR IsDateSelected =
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Month]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate])
			
			VAR slicerFilter =
			    FILTER(
			        ALLSELECTED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth
			    )
			
			RETURN
			SWITCH(
			    TRUE(),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "Absolute" && SelectedScenario = "AOP",
			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([SG&A NON Labor Varient AOP%], slicerFilter)
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "Absolute" && SelectedScenario = "FCST",
			    IF(IsDateSelected && NOT IsFullPeriod,
			        CALCULATE([SG&A NON Labor Varient FCST%], slicerFilter),
			        BLANK()
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "Absolute" && SelectedScenario = "YA",
			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([SG&A NON Labor Varient PY%], slicerFilter)
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "RPC" && SelectedScenario = "AOP",
			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([SG&A NON Labor Varient RPC AOP%], slicerFilter)
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "RPC" && SelectedScenario = "FCST",
			    IF(IsDateSelected && NOT IsFullPeriod,
			        CALCULATE([SG&A NON Labor Varient RPC FCST%], slicerFilter),
			        BLANK()
			    ),
			
			    SelectedToggle = "RPC" && SelectedScenario = "YA",
			    IF(IsDateSelected,
			        CALCULATE([SG&A NON Labor Varient RPC PY%], slicerFilter)
			    ),
			
			    BLANK()
			)
			
			
			
			```
		formatString: (#,##0%);#,##0%
		lineageTag: cd28dff8-d4ec-475a-9bca-bb2f0d4ec50b

		changedProperty = Name

		changedProperty = FormatString

	measure TSR = ```
			
			VAR SelectedTarget = SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics], "AOP")
			VAR Actual = [Revenue_TL]

			    SWITCH(
			    TRUE(),
			SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics]) = "AOP", [Quarter dynamic Revenue aop KPICARD],
			SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics]) = "FCST", [Quarter dynamic revenue FCST KPICARD],

			) 
			
			VAR PerformancePct = DIVIDE(Actual, Target)

			    IF(
			        ISBLANK(Target),
			        BLANK(),
			        IF(PerformancePct >= 1, "On Track", "Off Track")
			    )

	measure 'POG_Comp_Prior Period' = ```
			
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period_Op]
			
			var _isdsspw = 
			CALCULATE(
			    SUM(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[IsDSSVoid]),
			    REMOVEFILTERS(Operation_Cal_Day),
			    REMOVEFILTERS(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			    V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[Period]="PreviousWeek")
			
			var _dsspw = 
			CALCULATE(
			    SUM(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[IsDSS]),
			    REMOVEFILTERS(Operation_Cal_Day),
			    REMOVEFILTERS(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			    V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[Period]="PreviousWeek")
			
			var _val = DIVIDE(_isdsspw,_dsspw,BLANK()) 
			var _voidpw = IF(ISBLANK(_val),BLANK(),1-_val)
			
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('Operation_Cal_Day'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('Operation_Cal_Day'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			Var _PriorPeriod =
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        _isWeek, _voidpw,
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE([POG_Comp],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                            Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1))),
			        _isQuarter,CALCULATE([POG_Comp],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                             Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3)),
			                             FILTER(ALL(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail),
			                             V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[Period]="Monthly")),
			        _isYear,  CALCULATE([POG_Comp],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail),
			                             V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[Period]="Monthly"),
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                             Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			         )
			RETURN 
			IF(ISBLANK(_PriorPeriod)||SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay_Sort]) = 12.2, "NA",
			([POG_Comp]-_PriorPeriod)*100)
			```
		formatString: #,##0pts;(#,##0pts)
		displayFolder: POG
		lineageTag: 0127d0b4-7d13-480c-ab24-6090ef8b00f6

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isCustom":true}

	measure '%Sold_Prior Period' = ```
			
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period_Op]
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('Operation_Cal_Day'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('Operation_Cal_Day'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			Var _PriorPeriod =
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        _isWeek,CALCULATE([%Sold],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                            Operation_Cal_Day[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod - 7)),
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE([%Sold],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                            Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1))),
			        _isQuarter,CALCULATE([%Sold],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                             Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3))),
			        _isYear,  CALCULATE([%Sold],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                             Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			 )
			 
			RETURN ([%Sold] -_PriorPeriod)*100
			```
		formatString: #,##0pts;(#,##0pts)
		displayFolder: Rev
		lineageTag: 8d2d2d78-b036-42a3-965b-4a409361a4cf

	measure 'SKU_CMA_Prior Period' = ```
			
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			Var _PriorPeriod = 
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        _isWeek,CALCULATE([CMA_SKU_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod - 7)),
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE([CMA_SKU_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1))),
			        _isQuarter,CALCULATE([CMA_SKU_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3))),
			        _isYear,  CALCULATE([CMA_SKU_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			         )
			RETURN [CMA_SKU_Compliance]-_PriorPeriod
			```
		formatString: #,##0%;(#,##0%)
		displayFolder: CMA
		lineageTag: 9e42d2f0-722b-4cfc-b102-8549dd6cd395

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isCustom":true}

	measure IM_Selected_Period = ```
			
			 
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			RETURN
			SWITCH(
			    TRUE(),
			    _isWeek, [IM_Date Validation_Week],
			    _isMonth, [IM_Date Validation_Month],
			    _isQuarter,[IM_Date Validation_Quarter],
			    _isYear, [IM_Date Validation_Year],
			    BLANK()
			)
			 
			 
			/*
			SWITCH(
			    TRUE(),
			   _isWeek, VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[WeekStarting_ISO]),
			   _isMonth, VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfMonth]),
			   _isQuarter, VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]),
			    _isYear, VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]),
			    BLANK()
			)
			*/
			```
		formatString: General Date
		displayFolder: CMA
		lineageTag: 3961336c-cc6b-48e1-8b7f-1c72ec7dc9d9

	measure 'T1_CMA_Prior Period' = ```
			
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			Var _PriorPeriod =
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        _isWeek,CALCULATE([T1_CMA_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod - 7)),
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE([T1_CMA_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1))),
			        _isQuarter,CALCULATE([T1_CMA_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3))),
			        _isYear,  CALCULATE([T1_CMA_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			         )
			RETURN [T1_CMA_Compliance]-_PriorPeriod
			```
		formatString: #,##0%;(#,##0%)
		displayFolder: CMA
		lineageTag: de977793-083c-446a-a3f4-beaa019c9bdf

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isCustom":true}

	measure Cases_Per_Deliver_Adj_Vol_PY_CPH = ```
			var c22 = SUM(V_Fact_FB_Ops_CPH_CPC[DelvInvoicedQty])
			var d5 = 
			CALCULATE(
			    SUM(V_Fact_FB_Ops_CPH_CPC[DelvTotalOrder]),
			    SAMEPERIODLASTYEAR(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]))
			
			var c5 = 
			CALCULATE(
			    SUM(V_Fact_FB_Ops_CPH_CPC[DelvInvoicedQty]),
			    SAMEPERIODLASTYEAR(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]))
			var _e = SELECTEDVALUE(V_Fact_FB_Ops_CPH_CPC[DelvElasticity])
			
			var _val = 
			c22/((d5)*((((c22-c5)/c5)*_e)+1))
			
			return _val
			
			```
		displayFolder: Ops
		lineageTag: 6023b236-aa45-4e66-b255-0cfed5d44d82

			VAR a = 
			    CALCULATE(
			        SUM(V_FB_Financial_Management[AmtAOP]),
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] = "Total Operating Expense",
			        V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"}
			    )

			    CALCULATE(
			        SUM(V_FB_Financial_Management[AmtFcst39]),
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] = "Total Operating Expense",
			        V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"}
			    )
			
			VAR c = 
			    CALCULATE(
			        SUM(V_FB_Financial_Management[AmtFcst66]),
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] = "Total Operating Expense",
			        V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"}
			    )
			
			VAR d = 
			    CALCULATE(
			        SUM(V_FB_Financial_Management[AmtFcst93]),
			        V_Dim_FB_PlHier[PlHier] = "Total Operating Expense",
			        V_Dim_FB_Function[FnArea] IN {"Z009", "Z019"}
			    )
			
			VAR SelectedQuarters = VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter])
			
			VAR Result =
			    SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        COUNTROWS(SelectedQuarters) = 1 && 1 IN SelectedQuarters, a,
			        COUNTROWS(SelectedQuarters) = 1 && 2 IN SelectedQuarters, b,
			        COUNTROWS(SelectedQuarters) = 1 && 3 IN SelectedQuarters, c,
			        COUNTROWS(SelectedQuarters) = 1 && 4 IN SelectedQuarters, d,
			        SelectedQuarters = {1, 2}, a + b,
			        SelectedQuarters = {1, 3}, a + c,
			        SelectedQuarters = {1, 4}, a + d,
			        SelectedQuarters = {2, 3}, b + c,
			        SelectedQuarters = {2, 4}, b + d,
			        SelectedQuarters = {3, 4}, c + d,
			        SelectedQuarters = {1, 2, 3}, a + b + c,
			        SelectedQuarters = {2, 3, 4}, b + c + d,
			        SelectedQuarters = {1, 2, 3, 4}, a + b + c + d,
			        BLANK()
			    )
			
			RETURN Result
			
			```

	measure 'T2_CMA_Prior Period' = ```
			
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			Var _PriorPeriod =
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        _isWeek,CALCULATE([T2_CMA_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod - 7)),
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE([T2_CMA_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1))),
			        _isQuarter,CALCULATE([T2_CMA_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3))),
			        _isYear,  CALCULATE([T2_CMA_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			         )
			RETURN [T2_CMA_Compliance]-_PriorPeriod
			```

	measure Breakage_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops = ```
			
			 VAR TodayDate = TODAY()
			VAR CurrentMonthStart = DATE(YEAR(TodayDate), MONTH(TodayDate), 1)
			VAR DelayCutoff = CurrentMonthStart + 6  // 7th of the current month
			
			VAR MaxClosedMonth =
			    EOMONTH(TodayDate, IF(TodayDate < DelayCutoff, -2, -1))
			
			VAR CurrentYear = YEAR(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR CurrentMonth = MONTH(MaxClosedMonth)
			VAR VisualYear = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			VAR VisualQuarter = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter])
			VAR IsCurrentYear = VisualYear = CurrentYear
			
			VAR ExpectedMonths = IF(IsCurrentYear, CurrentMonth, 12)
			
			VAR SelectedMonths =
			    CALCULATETABLE(
			        VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = VisualYear
			    )
			
			VAR TotalMonthsSelected = COUNTROWS(SelectedMonths)
			VAR IsFullPeriod = TotalMonthsSelected = ExpectedMonths
			
			VAR IsDateSelected =
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Month]) ||
			    ISFILTERED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate])
			
			VAR MaxClosedQuarter =
			    CALCULATE(
			        MAX('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Quarter]),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth,
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = CurrentYear
			    )
			
			VAR IsClosedQuarter =
			    VisualYear < CurrentYear ||
			    (VisualYear = CurrentYear && VisualQuarter < MaxClosedQuarter)
			
			VAR slicerFilter =
			    FILTER(
			        ALLSELECTED('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[DayDate] <= MaxClosedMonth
			    )
			
			VAR MetricSelected = SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics])
			VAR BaseMeasure = [Breakage_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_final]
			VAR FilteredMeasure = CALCULATE(BaseMeasure, slicerFilter)
			
			RETURN
			    IF (
			        MetricSelected = "FCST",
			        IF (
			            IsDateSelected && NOT IsFullPeriod && NOT IsClosedQuarter,
			            IF(FilteredMeasure <> 0, FilteredMeasure, BLANK()),
			            BLANK()
			        ),
			        BaseMeasure
			    )
			/*IF(
			    SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics]) = "FCST",
			    IF(
			        MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber])<=6,"", [Breakage_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_final]),
			    [Breakage_Abs_RPC_Aops_FCST_YA_Attainment_Selection_Ops_final])*/
			    
			```

	measure 'Quarter FCST dynamic volume Bar' = ```
			VAR currentMonth = MONTH(TODAY())
			 
			RETURN
			SWITCH(
			    true(),
			    MAX('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber])<>currentMonth &&
			    MAX('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year]) = YEAR(TODAY())
			,
			CALCULATE(
			    [Volume_FCST_TL_nw],
			    KEEPFILTERS(
			        FILTER(
			            ALL('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] <> currentMonth &&
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = YEAR(TODAY())
			        )
			    ),FILTER(ALL('V_Fact_FB_Topline_Budget_All'[TimeGranularity],V_Fact_FB_Topline_Budget_All[RYBkt]),
			        V_Fact_FB_Topline_Budget_All[TimeGranularity] = "Monthly"
			)),
			 
			MAX('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber])=currentMonth
			     && MAX('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year]) = YEAR(TODAY()),
			     CALCULATE(
			    [Volume_FCST_TL_nw],
			    KEEPFILTERS(
			        FILTER(
			            ALL('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] = currentMonth
			                && 'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = YEAR(TODAY())
			        )
			    ),FILTER(ALL('V_Fact_FB_Topline_Budget_All'[TimeGranularity],V_Fact_FB_Topline_Budget_All[RYBkt]),
			        V_Fact_FB_Topline_Budget_All[TimeGranularity] = "Monthly"
			       &&  V_Fact_FB_Topline_Budget_All[RYBkt] IN {"RCY"}
			)))
			```

	measure 'Rate_Per_Case_fcst_TL KPICard' =

			VAR Volume = [Quarter dynamic Volume FCST KPICARD BLANK logic]
			
			RETURN
			    IF(
			        ISERROR(VALUE(Revenue)) || ISERROR(VALUE(Volume)) || Revenue = "" || Volume = "",
			        BLANK(),  // Return BLANK() if either Revenue or Volume is blank or non-numeric
			        DIVIDE(VALUE(Revenue), VALUE(Volume), 0)

	measure 'Quarter dynamic volume attainment aop' = ```
			
			VAR _yr = SELECTEDVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year])
			VAR _month = VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber])
			VAR _currentmonth = MONTH(TODAY())
			
			-- Actuals
			VAR _num =
			    CALCULATE (
			        SUM(V_Fact_FB_ToplineActuals_Summary[SalesCases])
			    )
			
			-- AOP for current month (if selected)
			VAR _D2 =
			    CALCULATE (
			        SUM(V_Fact_FB_Topline_Budget_All[SalesCasesBudget]),
			        REMOVEFILTERS(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			        FILTER (V_Dim_FB_CalDay,
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = _yr &&
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] = _currentmonth &&
			            _currentmonth IN _month
			        ),
			        
			        V_Fact_FB_Topline_Budget_All[TimeGranularity] = "MTD",
			        V_Fact_FB_Topline_Budget_All[RYBkt] = "RCY"
			        
			    )
			
			-- AOP for closed months (excluding current month)
			VAR _D3 =
			    CALCULATE (
			        SUM(V_Fact_FB_Topline_Budget_All[SalesCasesBudget]),
			        REMOVEFILTERS(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			        FILTER (
			            ('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = _yr &&
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] < _currentmonth &&
			            'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] IN _month
			        ),
			        
			        V_Fact_FB_Topline_Budget_All[TimeGranularity] = "Monthly"
			        
			    )
			
			VAR _den = _D2 + _D3
			
			RETURN
			if (_den = 0, BLANK(),
			
			DIVIDE(_num - _den, _den))
			
			    //DIVIDE((_num - _den), _den)
			```
		displayFolder: Topline
		lineageTag: dd0769ca-0d77-44dc-ba4e-6ebabdf97b78

	measure 'Quarter dynamic Revenue attainment YA' = ```
			
			//Quarter_Dynamic_Revenue_Variance :=
			VAR currentMonth = MONTH(TODAY())
			VAR currentYear = YEAR(TODAY())
			
			RETURN
			SUMX(
			    FILTER(
			        ADDCOLUMNS(
			            VALUES('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber]),
			            "YearVal", CALCULATE(MAX('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year]))
			        ),
			        [YearVal] = currentYear &&
			        'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] <= currentMonth
			    ),
			    VAR selectedMonth = 'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber]
			    VAR selectedYear = currentYear
			    VAR isCurrentMonth = selectedMonth = currentMonth
			
			    // ✅ Actuals
			    VAR actual =
			        CALCULATE(
			            [Revenue_TL],
			            FILTER(
			                ALL('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			                'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] = selectedMonth &&
			                'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = selectedYear
			            )
			        )
			
			    // ✅ Budget
			    VAR budget =
			        IF(
			            isCurrentMonth,
			            CALCULATE(
			                [Revenue_PY_TL],
			                FILTER(
			                    ALL('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			                    'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] = selectedMonth &&
			                    'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = selectedYear
			                ),
			                FILTER(
			                    ALL(V_Fact_FB_ToplineActuals_Summary[TimeGranularity]),
			                    V_Fact_FB_ToplineActuals_Summary[TimeGranularity] = "Pv MTD"
			                )
			            ),
			            CALCULATE(
			                [Revenue_PY_TL],
			                FILTER(
			                    ALL('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'),
			                    'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthNumber] = selectedMonth &&
			                    'V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[Year] = selectedYear
			                ),
			                FILTER(
			                    ALL(V_Fact_FB_ToplineActuals_Summary[TimeGranularity]),
			                    V_Fact_FB_ToplineActuals_Summary[TimeGranularity] = "Monthly"
			                )
			            )
			        )
			
			    // ✅ Return % variance: (Actual - Budget) / Budget
			    RETURN DIVIDE(actual - budget, budget)
			)
			
			```
		displayFolder: Topline
		lineageTag: c6f04de1-b679-4da2-aa76-b72e190108c7

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isGeneralNumber":true}

	measure 1T = ```
			
			var _yr = SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[Year])

			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber]<_currentmonth,
			    V_Fact_FB_ToplineActuals_Summary[TimeGranularity] = "Monthly"

	measure '3y dummy' = ```
			
			VAR _yr = SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[Year])
			VAR _selectedMonths = VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber])
			VAR _currentMonth = MONTH(TODAY())
			
			VAR _num = [Rate_per_Case_TL]
			
			-- Pv MTD for Current Month Last Year
			VAR _D2 =
			IF (
			    _currentMonth IN _selectedMonths,
			    CALCULATE(
			        [Rate_per_Case_TL],
			        FILTER(
			            ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[Year] = _yr - 1 &&
			            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber] = _currentMonth
			        ),
			        V_Fact_FB_ToplineActuals_Summary[TimeGranularity] = "Pv MTD"
			    ),
			    0
			)
			
			-- Closed Months from Selection
			VAR _closedMonths =
			    FILTER(
			        _selectedMonths,
			        V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber] < _currentMonth
			    )
			
			-- Monthly for Closed Months Last Year
			VAR _D3 =
			IF (
			    COUNTROWS(_closedMonths) > 0,
			    CALCULATE(
			        [Rate_per_Case_TL],
			        FILTER(
			            ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[Year] = _yr - 1 &&
			            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber] IN _closedMonths
			        ),
			        V_Fact_FB_ToplineActuals_Summary[TimeGranularity] = "Monthly"
			    ),
			    0
			)
			
			-- Combine Denominator
			VAR _den = _D2 + _D3
			
			-- Final Output
			RETURN
			DIVIDE((_num - _den), _den)
			
			```
		displayFolder: Topline
		lineageTag: 1a22923c-6848-4e69-8a05-1db1c558fb3d

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isGeneralNumber":true}

			        "TeaSold",SUM(V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TeaJCSkuSold]),
			         "WaterPromo", MAX(V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[WaterPromo]),
			        "WaterSold",SUM(V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[WaterSkuSold])
			    ),
			    if ((
			    if ([CSDSold]>=[CSDPromo],1,0) + 
			    if ([SPSold]>=[SPPromo],1,0) +
			    if ([EnergySold]>=[EnergyPromo],1,0) +
			    if ([TeaSold]>=[TeaPromo],1,0) +
			    if ([WaterSold]>=[WaterPromo],1,0) )>=5,1,0)
			)
			```
		formatString: 0
		displayFolder: CMA_Account
		lineageTag: fce79485-779d-4267-b848-5220347e78a3

	measure 'CMA_Account_Prior Period' = ```
			
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			Var _PriorPeriod = 
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        _isWeek,CALCULATE([Account_CMA_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod - 7)),
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE([Account_CMA_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1))),
			        _isQuarter,CALCULATE([Account_CMA_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3))),
			        _isYear,  CALCULATE([Account_CMA_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			         )
			RETURN [Account_CMA_Compliance]-_PriorPeriod
			```
		formatString: #,##0%;(#,##0%)
		displayFolder: CMA_Account
		lineageTag: 023e3fcb-88a9-4bda-bf68-b2f4531f61c3

	measure 'CMA_SKU_Prior Period' = ```
			
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			Var _PriorPeriod = 
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        _isWeek,CALCULATE([CMA_SKU_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod - 7)),
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE([CMA_SKU_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1))),
			        _isQuarter,CALCULATE([CMA_SKU_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3))),
			        _isYear,  CALCULATE([CMA_SKU_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			         )
			RETURN [CMA_SKU_Compliance]-_PriorPeriod
			```
		formatString: #,##0%;(#,##0%)
		displayFolder: CMA_SKU
		lineageTag: b1d11d80-bf90-4597-8113-8af939632404

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isCustom":true}

	measure CMA_SKU_Compliance_tgl =
			
			Var _Category = SELECTEDVALUE(CMA_Category_Selector[CMA_SKU_Category])
			
			Var _SKU_Target = SWITCH(TRUE(),
			_Category="Total CMA",[SKU_CMA_Compliance],
			_Category="CSD",[CSD_SKU_CMA_Compliance],
			_Category="ENERGY",[Energy_SKU_CMA_Compliance],
			_Category="SPORT",[Sports_SKU_CMA_Compliance],
			_Category="TEA & JC",[TeanJC_SKU_CMA_Compliance],
			_Category="WATER",[Water_SKU_CMA_Compliance]
			)
			RETURN _SKU_Target

	measure 'CMA_SKU_Prior Period_tgl' = ```
			
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period_Op]
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('Operation_Cal_Day'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('Operation_Cal_Day'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			Var _PriorPeriod = 
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        _isWeek,CALCULATE([CMA_SKU_Compliance_tgl],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                            Operation_Cal_Day[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod - 7)),
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE([CMA_SKU_Compliance_tgl],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                            Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1))),
			        _isQuarter,CALCULATE([CMA_SKU_Compliance_tgl],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                             Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3))),
			        _isYear,  CALCULATE([CMA_SKU_Compliance_tgl],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                             Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			         )
			RETURN 
			IF(ISBLANK(_PriorPeriod),"NA",([CMA_SKU_Compliance_tgl] - _PriorPeriod)*100)
			```
		formatString: #,##0pts;(#,##0pts)
		displayFolder: CMA_SKU
		lineageTag: 68f65036-7b4c-4b21-a8be-17cdace796c1

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isCustom":true}

	measure '%Display_schdls_tobe_Built_SF_Prior Period' = ```
			
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period_Op]
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('Operation_Cal_Day'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('Operation_Cal_Day'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			Var _PriorPeriod =
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        _isWeek,CALCULATE([Displays Schedules to be Built],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                            Operation_Cal_Day[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod - 7)),
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE([Displays Schedules to be Built],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                            Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1))),
			        _isQuarter,CALCULATE([Displays Schedules to be Built],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                             Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3))),
			        _isYear,  CALCULATE([Displays Schedules to be Built],
			                            FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			                             Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			 )
			 
			RETURN ([Displays Schedules to be Built] -_PriorPeriod)*100
			
			```

	measure 'Displays_Pending_Prior Period' = ```
			
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&

			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])

			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])

			        TRUE(),

			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod - 7)),
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE([Displays Pending],

			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			 )

	measure 'SKU Opportunity' = ```
			
			
			// This dax will calculate the YTD, QYD, MTD CMA based on the date slicer selected.
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			Var Opp = [Total_Variance]
			
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			Var Avg_Opp =
			CALCULATE(
			        AVERAGEX(
			            VALUES(V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[PeriodEnd]),
			            [Total_Variance]
			                ),
			            V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TimeGranularity]="Monthly"||
			            V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TimeGranularity]="Current Week"
			        )    
			
			Var _SelectedKPI = 
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        _isWeek,CALCULATE(AVERAGEX(
			                             VALUES(V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TimeGranularity]),
			                             [Total_Variance]
			                                     ),
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod)),
			
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE(AVERAGEX(VALUES(V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TimeGranularity]),
			                             [Total_Variance]
			                                    ),
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfMonth]=_SelectedPeriod),
			                            V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TimeGranularity]="Monthly"||
			                            V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TimeGranularity]="Current Week"
			                        ),
			                         
			        _isQuarter,CALCULATE(Avg_Opp,
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]=_SelectedPeriod)),
			                             
			        _isYear,  CALCULATE(Avg_Opp,
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod), MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			         )
			RETURN _SelectedKPI
			```
		formatString: #,0
		displayFolder: CMA SKU
		lineageTag: 22bfc53b-5333-45bd-a4e0-876f2d691fb5
