	measure Requested_Deliveries_Prior_Period_abs = ```
			
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			
			var _maxdate1 = MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate])
			var _mindate1 = MIN(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate])
			var _x = DATEDIFF(_mindate1,_maxdate1,DAY)
			
			var 
			_isWeek_val = 
			    CALCULATE(SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOPORDERS[TotalOrder]),
			     FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			     Operation_Cal_Day[DayDate]>=_mindate1 - 7&&
			     Operation_Cal_Day[DayDate]<=_mindate1-7+_x))
			    // CALCULATE(SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOPORDERS[TotalOrder]),
			    //  FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			    //  Operation_Cal_Day[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod - 7))
			
			var _isMonth_val = 
			    CALCULATE(SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOPORDERS[TotalOrder]),
			     FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			     Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1)))
			
			var 
			_iscurrmonth_val = 
			    CALCULATE(
			        SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOPORDERS[TotalOrder]),
			         FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			         Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1)),
			         DAY(Operation_Cal_Day[DayDate])<=DAY(MAX(Operation_Cal_Day[DayDate])))
			
			var 
			_isQuarter_val = 
			    CALCULATE(SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOPORDERS[TotalOrder]),
			     FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			     V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3)),
			     V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]<=MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]))
			
			// CurrentQuartercal
			var prev_q = STARTOFQUARTER(DATEADD(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate],-1,QUARTER))
			
			var prev_q_end = ENDOFQUARTER(DATEADD(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate],-1,QUARTER))
			
			var curr_q_start = STARTOFQUARTER(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate])
			
			var _maxdate = MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate])
			
			var _isquarter_curr_val = 
			CALCULATE(
			    SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOPORDERS[TotalOrder]),
			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]>=prev_q && 
			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate] <= IF(
			                                prev_q_end <= prev_q + DATEDIFF(curr_q_start,_maxdate,DAY),
			                                prev_q_end,prev_q + DATEDIFF(curr_q_start,_maxdate,DAY
			                                )
			    ))
			
			var 
			_isYear_val =  
			    CALCULATE(SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOPORDERS[TotalOrder]),
			    FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))),
			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]<=MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[LYDayDate]))
			
			var _z = 
			SWITCH(
			       TRUE(),
			        _x<7, _isWeek_val,
			        _x<=30&&MONTH(TODAY()) in VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber])&&HASONEVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]), _iscurrmonth_val,
			        _x<=92&&MONTH(TODAY()) in VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber]), _isquarter_curr_val,
			        _x<=30, _isMonth_val,
			        _x<=92, _isQuarter_val,
			         _isYear_val)
			
			RETURN _z
			```
		displayFolder: Ops - DNP
		lineageTag: ad25fc82-e730-4725-ac2b-841e4943d6ae

			        _x<=92, _isQuarter_val,
			         _isYear_val)

	measure Haulback_cases_PriorPeriod_abs =

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isGeneralNumber":true}

	measure Haulback_cases_PriorPeriod_den = ```
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			
			var _maxdate1 = MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate])
			var _mindate1 = MIN(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate])
			var _x = DATEDIFF(_mindate1,_maxdate1,DAY)
			
			var 
			_isWeek_val = 
			    CALCULATE(SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOP[COPA_SALES_QTY]),
			     FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			     Operation_Cal_Day[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod - 7))
			
			var _isMonth_val = 
			    CALCULATE(SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOP[COPA_SALES_QTY]),
			     FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			     Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1)))
			
			var 
			_iscurrmonth_val = 
			    CALCULATE(
			        SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOP[COPA_SALES_QTY]),
			         FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			         Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1)),
			         DAY(Operation_Cal_Day[DayDate])<=DAY(MAX(Operation_Cal_Day[DayDate])))
			
			var 
			_isQuarter_val = 
			    CALCULATE(SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOP[COPA_SALES_QTY]),
			     FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			     V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3)),
			     V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]<=MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]))
			
			// CurrentQuartercal
			var prev_q = STARTOFQUARTER(DATEADD(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate],-1,QUARTER))
			
			var prev_q_end = ENDOFQUARTER(DATEADD(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate],-1,QUARTER))
			
			var curr_q_start = STARTOFQUARTER(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate])
			
			var _maxdate = MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate])
			
			var _isquarter_curr_val = 
			CALCULATE(
			    SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOP[COPA_SALES_QTY]),
			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]>=prev_q && 
			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate] <= IF(
			                                prev_q_end <= prev_q + DATEDIFF(curr_q_start,_maxdate,DAY),
			                                prev_q_end,prev_q + DATEDIFF(curr_q_start,_maxdate,DAY
			                                )
			    ))
			
			var 
			_isYear_val =  
			    CALCULATE(SUM(V_FACT_FB_OPS_ROLLEDSTOP[COPA_SALES_QTY]),
			    FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))),
			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]<=MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[LYDayDate]))
			
			var _z = 
			SWITCH(
			       TRUE(),
			        _x<7, _isWeek_val,
			        _x<=30&&MONTH(TODAY()) in VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber])&&HASONEVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]), _iscurrmonth_val,
			        _x<=92&&MONTH(TODAY()) in VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber]), _isquarter_curr_val,
			        _x<=30, _isMonth_val,
			        _x<=92, _isQuarter_val,
			         _isYear_val)
			
			RETURN _z
			```
		displayFolder: Ops - DNP
		lineageTag: cd0fe4df-9a34-4839-9258-fe8e4992d7ef

	measure SKU_CMA_Comp =

			   [Total_Promo]-

		displayFolder: CMA_SKU

	measure CSD_SKU_CMA_Comp =

	measure CSD_SKU_CMA_Compliance = ```
			
			// This dax will calculate the YTD, QYD, MTD CMA based on the date slicer selected.
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			Var Avg_CMA =
			CALCULATE(
			        AVERAGEX(
			            VALUES(V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[Period]),
			            [CSD_SKU_CMA_Comp]
			                ),
			            V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TimeGranularity]="Monthly"||
			            V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TimeGranularity]="Current Week"
			        )    
			
			Var _SelectedKPI = 
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        _isWeek,CALCULATE(AVERAGEX(
			                             VALUES(V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TimeGranularity]),
			                             [CSD_SKU_CMA_Comp]
			                                     ),
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod)),
			
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE(AVERAGEX(VALUES(V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TimeGranularity]),
			                             [CSD_SKU_CMA_Comp]
			                                    ),
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfMonth]=_SelectedPeriod),
			                            V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TimeGranularity]="Monthly"||
			                            V_Fact_FB_CMAComplianceSummary[TimeGranularity]="Current Week"
			                        ),
			                         
			        _isQuarter,CALCULATE(Avg_CMA,
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]=_SelectedPeriod)),
			                             
			        _isYear,  CALCULATE(Avg_CMA,
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod), MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			         )
			RETURN _SelectedKPI
			```
		formatString: 0%;-0%;0%
		displayFolder: CMA_SKU
		lineageTag: fe28181d-f87b-4af8-9ef6-14896289cb9c

			        _isYear,  CALCULATE(Avg_CMA,
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod), MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))

	measure %Sold_Selected = ```
			
			
			// This dax will calculate the YTD, QYD, MTD CMA based on the date slicer selected.
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])

			CALCULATE(
			        AVERAGEX(
			            VALUES(V_Fact_FB_RevDetail[Time Granularity]),
			            [%Sold_Base_Calc]
			                ),
			                CONTAINSSTRING(V_Fact_FB_RevDetail[Time Granularity],"Monthly")||
			                CONTAINSSTRING(V_Fact_FB_RevDetail[Time Granularity],"Current Week")
			        )

			        TRUE(),

			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),

			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),

			                            CONTAINSSTRING(V_Fact_FB_RevDetail[Time Granularity],"Monthly")||
			                            CONTAINSSTRING(V_Fact_FB_RevDetail[Time Granularity],"Current Week")

	measure %Void_Base_Calc = ```
			
			var _x = SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay_Sort])
			var _dssvoid = 
			CALCULATE(
			    SUM(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[IsDSSVoid]),
			    V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[Period]="PreviousWeek")
			var _dss = 
			CALCULATE(
			    SUM(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[IsDSS]),
			    V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[Period]="PreviousWeek")
			    
			var _dssvoidall = SUM(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[IsDSSVoid])-_dssvoid
			var _dssall = SUM(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[IsDSS])-_dss
			
			var _prevwk = 
			DIVIDE(_dssvoid,_dss)
			var _all = 
			DIVIDE(_dssvoidall,_dssall)
			
			RETURN
			SWITCH(_x,
			    12.2,
			    _prevwk,
			    _all)
			```
		formatString: 0%;-0%;0%
		displayFolder: POG
		lineageTag: 0cfe5cee-b798-4905-8baa-8d32e6f55825

	measure Cases_Per_Delivery_Change_vs_YA_CPH_matrix_LP =
			
			VAR TodayDate = TODAY()
			VAR CurrentMonthStart = DATE(YEAR(TodayDate), MONTH(TodayDate), 1)
			VAR DelayCutoff = CurrentMonthStart + 6
			RETURN
			CALCULATE(
			IF([Cases_Per_Deliver_actuals_CPH_matrix_LP]<>0 ,
			DIVIDE([Cases_Per_Deliver_actuals_CPH_matrix_LP]-[Cases_Per_Deliver_actuals_PY_CPH_matrix_LP],[Cases_Per_Deliver_actuals_PY_CPH_matrix_LP],0)," "),
			    FILTER(
			        VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]),
			        (YEAR(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]) = YEAR(TODAY()) && MONTH(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]) < (MONTH(TODAY())-1)) ||
			        (YEAR(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]) = YEAR(TODAY()) && MONTH(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]) < MONTH(TODAY())
			        && TODAY()>DelayCutoff)
			    )
			)
		formatString: (#,##0%);#,##0%
		displayFolder: Ops
		lineageTag: c348ec0d-c883-4b07-9874-589a4154a4e3

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isCustom":true}

			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			Var _PriorPeriod =
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			        _isWeek,CALCULATE([%Sold_Base_Calc],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[WeekStarting_ISO]=_SelectedPeriod - 7)),
			        _isMonth,CALCULATE([%Sold_Base_Calc],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1))),
			        _isQuarter,CALCULATE([%Sold_Base_Calc],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3))),
			        _isYear,  CALCULATE([%Sold_Base_Calc],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			         )
			RETURN [%Sold_Base_Calc]-_PriorPeriod
			```
		formatString: #,##0%;(#,##0%)
		displayFolder: Rev
		lineageTag: 8bc63fd6-495f-4190-a7cb-de2cd0c5d24e

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isCustom":true}

	measure Haulback_cases_table_prior_period_abs = ```
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			
			var _maxdate1 = MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate])
			var _mindate1 = MIN(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate])
			var _x = DATEDIFF(_mindate1,_maxdate1,DAY)
			
			var 
			_isWeek_val = 
			    CALCULATE([Haulback_cases_table],
			     FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			     Operation_Cal_Day[DayDate]>=_mindate1 - 7&&
			     Operation_Cal_Day[DayDate]<=_mindate1-7+_x))
			
			var _isMonth_val = 
			    CALCULATE([Haulback_cases_table],
			     FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			     Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1)))
			
			var 
			_iscurrmonth_val = 
			    CALCULATE(
			        [Haulback_cases_table],
			         FILTER(ALL(Operation_Cal_Day),
			         Operation_Cal_Day[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1)),
			         DAY(Operation_Cal_Day[DayDate])<=DAY(MAX(Operation_Cal_Day[DayDate])))
			
			var 
			_isQuarter_val = 
			    CALCULATE([Haulback_cases_table],
			     FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			     V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3)),
			     V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]<=MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]))
			
			// CurrentQuartercal
			var prev_q = STARTOFQUARTER(DATEADD(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate],-1,QUARTER))
			
			var prev_q_end = ENDOFQUARTER(DATEADD(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate],-1,QUARTER))
			
			var curr_q_start = STARTOFQUARTER(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate])
			
			var _maxdate = MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate])
			
			var _isquarter_curr_val = 
			CALCULATE(
			    [Haulback_cases_table],
			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]>=prev_q && 
			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate] <= prev_q + DATEDIFF(curr_q_start,_maxdate,DAY))
			
			var 
			_isYear_val =  
			    CALCULATE([Haulback_cases_table],
			    FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))),
			    V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]<=MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[LYDayDate]))
			
			var _z = 
			SWITCH(
			       TRUE(),
			        _x<7, _isWeek_val,
			        _x<=30&&MONTH(TODAY()) in VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber])&&HASONEVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]), _iscurrmonth_val,
			        _x<=92&&MONTH(TODAY()) in VALUES(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[MonthNumber]), _isquarter_curr_val,
			        _x<=30, _isMonth_val,
			        _x<=92, _isQuarter_val,
			         _isYear_val)
			
			RETURN _z
			```
		displayFolder: Ops - DNP
		lineageTag: b02d35eb-1df5-4948-82d4-277e6ac7da57

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isGeneralNumber":true}

	measure Selected_timeperiod = ```
			
			
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[MonthName]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			
			Var sel_TP = 
			SWITCH(TRUE(),
			_isWeek,"Week",
			_isMonth,"Month",
			_isQuarter,"Quarter",
			_isYear,"Year"
			)
			
			RETURN sel_TP
			```
		lineageTag: 6a71833d-775b-461b-8955-0307b652e7f8

	measure 'CMA_SKU_Prior Period_SP' = ```
			
			var _SelectedPeriod=[IM_Selected_Period]
			VAR Seltp = [Selected_timeperiod]
			
			Var _PriorPeriod = 
			 SWITCH(
			        TRUE(),
			       
			       Seltp= "Month",CALCULATE([CMA_Dynamic_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                            V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfMonth]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -1))),
			        Seltp="Quarter",CALCULATE([CMA_Dynamic_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfQuarter]=EDATE(_SelectedPeriod, -3))),
			       Seltp= "Year",  CALCULATE([CMA_Dynamic_Compliance],
			                            FILTER(ALL(V_Dim_FB_CalDay),
			                             V_Dim_FB_CalDay[FirstDayOfYear]= DATE(YEAR(_SelectedPeriod) - 1, MONTH(_SelectedPeriod), DAY(_SelectedPeriod))))
			         )
			RETURN 
			//([CMA_Dynamic_Compliance] - _PriorPeriod)*100
			ROUND([CMA_Dynamic_Compliance],2)*100-ROUND(_PriorPeriod,2)*100
			```
		formatString: #,##0pts;(#,##0pts)

	measure Notblank = ```
			
			VAR CurrentMonthNumber = MONTH(TODAY())
			VAR SelectedMonthNumber = MONTH(MAX(V_Dim_FB_CalDay[DayDate]))
			VAR IsFilteredRetailer = 
			    ISFILTERED(V_Dim_FB_CustChainHeir[NationalChainName]) 
			    || ISFILTERED(V_Dim_FB_CustChainHeir[TerritoryName])
			    || ISFILTERED(V_Dim_FB_CustChainHeir[BranchName])
			    || ISFILTERED(V_Dim_FB_CustChainHeir[SalesGroupName])
			VAR SelectedMetric = SELECTEDVALUE('Metric Table'[Metrics])
			
			RETURN
			SWITCH(
			    TRUE(),
			    SelectedMetric = "AOP" &&
			    (
			        (NOT IsFilteredRetailer || SelectedMonthNumber <= CurrentMonthNumber)
			        && ( NOT ISBLANK([Quarter dynamic volume AOP bar]) || NOT ISBLANK([Quarter dynamic revenue AOP bar]))
			    ), 1,
			
			    SelectedMetric IN {"FCST", "YA"} &&
			    ( NOT ISBLANK([Quarter dynamic volume AOP bar]) || NOT ISBLANK([Quarter dynamic revenue AOP bar])), 1,
			
			    0
			)
			
			
			```

	measure IM_Selected_Period_Op = ```
			
			 
			VAR _isWeek =
			    CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			     HASONEVALUE('Operation_Cal_Day'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			     HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isMonth =
			    Not CONTAINSSTRING(SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay]),"Week") &&
			    HASONEVALUE('Operation_Cal_Day'[YearMonthDay]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isQuarter =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[QuarterID]) &&
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			VAR _isYear =
			    HASONEVALUE('V_Dim_FB_CalDay'[YearID])
			 
			RETURN
			SWITCH(
			    TRUE(),
			    _isWeek, [IM_Date Validation_Week],
			    _isMonth, [IM_Date Validation_Month],
			    _isQuarter,[IM_Date Validation_Quarter],
			    _isYear, [IM_Date Validation_Year],
			    BLANK()
			)
			
			```
		formatString: General Date
		displayFolder: CMA
		lineageTag: 719a1d8a-6923-442d-8a89-ce96ac66bf05

	measure IsDSSVoid = ```
			
			var _tp = SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay_Sort])
			
			var _pw = 
			CALCULATE(
			    SUM(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[IsDSSVoid]),
			    V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[Period]="PreviousWeek")
			
			var _den = DISTINCTCOUNT(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[Monthnumber])
			
			var _all = SUM(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[IsDSSVoid])-_pw
			
			RETURN
			SWITCH(_tp,
			    12.2,
			    _pw,
			    DIVIDE(_all, _den))
			```
		displayFolder: POG
		lineageTag: 2086f917-9689-44d2-bbd6-d49514fc6fb0

		annotation PBI_FormatHint = {"isGeneralNumber":true}

	measure IsDSSVoid_NewItem = ```
			
			var _tp = SELECTEDVALUE(Operation_Cal_Day[YearMonthDay_Sort])
			
			var _pw = 
			CALCULATE(
			    SUM(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[IsDSSVoid]),
			    V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[Period]="PreviousWeek",
			    V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[POGItemType]="NEW ITEM")
			
			var _den = DISTINCTCOUNT(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[monthnumber])
			
			var _all = 
			CALCULATE(
			    SUM(V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[IsDSSVoid]),
			    V_Fact_FB_POGVoidDetail[POGItemType]="NEW ITEM") -_pw
			
			RETURN
			SWITCH(_tp,
			    12.2,
			    _pw,
			    DIVIDE(_all, _den))
			```
		formatString: #,0
		displayFolder: POG
		lineageTag: 5af5971b-17f2-48c2-8d91-cdf94dae2cc5
